In verse 19, he describes the puruSha in relation to shiva thus:

He who is this actor of this world play is shambhu, who is pure consciousness.
His state imbued with the many disguises taken by the actor is indeed that which becomes the puruSha.
(Does anyone recognize a meter here??)
